Network & PCP,MATIS | PROD | BCBSMI | Eligibility - New Patient creation when another patient with the same Member ID already exists,"BCBSMI has a requirement to support possibility to assign one Member ID to multiple patients, e.g. family members. === SHEET: Eligibility_Confluence ===
"OncoHealth integrates eligibility data from health plans (“payers”) to determine whether members have valid coverage and to drive workflows such as prior authorization, benefit checks and letter generation. The platform uses an ETL process to ingest files supplied by each payer, stores the data in a fortify database, and exposes it through the Eligibility API and MATIS UI. Standard functionality is shared across all payers, but additional rules are configured for specific plans.",,
,,
,,
,,
,,
Onboarding prerequisites for new payers. ,,
"When a new payer signs up, several steps must be completed before eligibility verification can go live:

- Payer configuration – Using the Add/Edit Payer UI, the implementations team sets up the payer’s required settings, maps lines of business (LOBs) and configures decision‑logic parameters. Drug lists, drug rules and enhanced TAT (turnaround time) configurations are loaded at the same time. Providers must be loaded into provider databases, Salesforce and the OADB, and payer‑specific source flags (e.g., “G” for GEIS) are configured. Member records are uploaded to the eligibility database.

- Secondary items – Letter templates and notification settings, outbound authorization (EOD) file configuration, and drug formulary data are set up. These items may be manually uploaded if the payer approves. MessageBridge routing rules ensure that member letters/faxes are delivered to the mailing vendor, and optional SFTP destinations can be added when payers require copies of member letters.",,
,,
,,
,,
,,
,,
Eligibility data ingestion and staging,,
Eligibility data arrives in 13 files for each payer. The core files and their staging tables are:,,
File,Purpose and DB table,Notes
HF_Members,Loaded into fortify.STG_Members via fnHFMembers and fnHFMemberDeactivation,"Contains member demographic data; unique by (InsuranceProviderID, MemberID) via patientIdent. Deactivation file terminates members because the main file lacks effective/term dates."
HF_Eligibility,Loaded into fortify.STG_Eligibility via fnHFEligibility,"Contains coverage data; unique by (InsuranceProviderID, MemberID, MajorLineOfBusiness, CoverageStartDate) using eligibilityIdent."
HF_EligibilityFlags_boolean / HF_EligibilityFlags,Loaded into fortify.STG_EligibilityFlags via fnHFEligibilityFlags_bool and fnHFEligibilityFlags_nonbool,"Holds additional eligibility attributes (e.g., dual‑eligibility, out‑of‑area benefits). Boolean flags missing in the file are treated as “no,” while list/text flags missing result in blank values."
"HF_Carriers, HF_Plans, HF_Networks, HF_CarrierNetworks, HF_NetworkSecondaryNetworkMapping","Loaded into various fortify staging tables (Carrier, STG_Plans, STG_HFNetworks, STG_HFCarrierNetworks)","Define carriers, plans, networks, and secondary/fallback networks used for provider selection. The secondary‑network mapping file allows members in a primary network to access providers in a fallback network."
,,
,,
Staging pipeline,,
"A Prefect pipeline called fortify‑build‑elig runs whenever new files are present for a payer enabled for eligibility loading. It executes three data flows sequentially:

1. Stage_Members: Calls stored procedure lvl2.usp_Fortify_SelectMembers with an ExecutionID. Steps:

 - Looks up each row’s preferred language from fortify.MemberLanguageXWalk.

 - Deduplicates members by patientIdent (keeps the record with the latest coverage end date).

 - Computes a hash of each row for change tracking.

-  Merges records into fortify.STG_Members.

2. Stage_Eligibility: Calls stored procedure lvl2.usp_Fortify_SelectEligibility. Steps:

 - Performs PCP (primary care provider) lookup using methods defined per payer.

 - Overrides network for payers that do not perform network checks.

 - For Excellus plans, it looks up the plan in fortify.PlanCarrierXWalk.

 - Deduplicates eligibility records by eligibilityIdent (latest coverage end date).

 - Hashes rows and merges into fortify.STG_Eligibility.

3. Stage_Eligibility_Flags: Calls lvl2.usp_Fortify_SelectEligibilityFlags. This flow has a branch for each flag, filters eligible rows and generates a flag for each record that should have it, then combines and deduplicates the flags before merging into fortify.STG_EligibilityFlags.",,
,,
Extraction to application,,
"After staging, the data is extracted into the application layer, where it supports real‑time eligibility verification and case management:

1. Eligibility API – Provides a 270/271‑style interface that returns member coverage and flags when MATIS or external users request eligibility. The API uses values from the eligibility database and returns error codes if data is missing. For example, the Dual Eligibility enhancement adds dualEligibilityStatus and planType fields to the API response.

2. MATIS UI – When a user starts a prior authorization or edits eligibility, MATIS calls the API to display the member’s coverage, network status, dual eligibility, and other flags. The UI shows fields such as Member Benefit (Medical and Pharmacy, Medical, Pharmacy) and separate Medical Benefit/Pharmacy Benefit statuses.

3. Workflow rules – Eligibility data drives recommended actions. If a member lacks a benefit, OneUM marks protocols as out‑of‑scope, generates letters, and sets statuses accordingly. Out‑of‑area and out‑of‑network flags, dual‑eligibility status and other flags can also drive letter language or network selection.",,
,,
,,
Function Area,Shared Standard Behavior,Payer-Specific Customizations
Eligibility Data Ingestion,"13 files (Members, Eligibility, Flags, Carriers, Plans, Networks etc.); ETL with Stage_Members, Stage_Eligibility, Stage_Eligibility_Flags; dedupe & hash; PCP and network lookup",Excellus: Plan mapping using PlanCarrierXWalk; BCBSMI: groups w/out pharmacy benefits flagged via CAG; GEIS: source flag G
Benefit Indicators,Assumes both Medical & Pharmacy benefits; UI shows Member Benefit dropdown and separate Medical/Pharmacy benefit fields,BCBSMI & Sentara: add HasMedicalBenefits/HasPharmacyBenefits fields; OOS logic for missing benefits; custom letter messages
Eligibility Flags,Supports flags (boolean or list) stored in EligibilityFlag tables; used for additional info,"Devoted: Dual Eligibility status (F/P/N); HPHC/GHP: Out-of-Area, Out-of-Network flags; future custom flags"
Network & PCP Checks,PCP lookup by payer; network overridden for payers w/o network checks; fallback network mapping for OON selection,None specified beyond standard fallback mapping; Excellus network configuration; some payers skip network checks
Dual Eligibility / DSNP,Not applicable; only some plans require,Devoted (DSNP): track DualEligibilityStatus & ProductType; add fields to API & UI; dynamic fax content
Letters & Dynamic Notifications,Dynamic fax content with configurable variables; letter templates loaded per payer; out-of-scope messages drive determination column,Dual eligibility: DSNP-specific appeal language; BCBSMI/Sentara: Out-of-scope member benefit messages; dynamic variable ~HelpInfo for DSNP
Re-verification & Overrides,Eligibility re-verification before case submission; CRS can override eligibility during outages,"Incident example: HMWC, FMHP, TripleS re-verification bug fixed via mapping correction; no unique payer logic"

=== SHEET: Eligibility_ado_tickets_categor ===


=== SHEET: BKBS_Eligibility Data ===
Requirements Summary,Description,Acceptance criteria,Notes
Field name alignment,"Ensure the production eligibility file uses field names that match the agreed layout; extra fields (Drug Formulary Name, Carve Out indicator and dates) must be documented and mapped",All fields in the eligibility file correspond to the layout; extra fields are either removed or mapped; no unknown fields or placeholder rows; final row does not contain null values,Test files had field names that did not match the expected layout and contained extra fields such as Drug Formulary Name and Prescription Benefit Carve Out indicator/dates
Prescription benefit carve-out handling,Implement support for the prescription benefit carve-out indicator and its effective and termination dates to determine when a member’s PBM is Optum versus an alternate PBM,"When the Carve Out indicator is Y, the effective and termination dates are populated; PBM routing logic respects these dates; when indicator is N, Optum remains the PBM",The carve-out indicator identifies whether prescription benefits are carved out of Optum; these fields explain when Optum is not the PBM of record
Drug formulary linkage,Include the Drug Formulary Name/ID in the eligibility file to link members to the correct formulary for drug coverage determination,Each member record contains a valid formulary identifier linking to the PBM formulary table and is used in drug coverage checks,The Drug Formulary Name field links the member to the formulary so that OncoHealth can determine which drugs/products are on the member’s formulary
Test file representativeness & data quality,Ensure sample and production files include all necessary combinations of product types and benefit indicators and address missing provider network IDs,"Production data contains all product types (e.g., PPO, EPO, COMHMO) and covers members with and without drug coverage; provider network ID is populated where applicable; data quality checks confirm representativeness of the sample",Profiler reports showed limited combinations and missing network IDs; additional product types may be introduced and COMHMO lacked network ID in test extracts
Secure automated ingestion & validation,"Build a secure, automated pipeline to ingest eligibility and demographic files from BlueKC’s SFTP, validate them, transform them to Bronze/Silver/Gold/EligibilityMS layers and route them to UM systems",Scheduled jobs pick up files from SFTP; successful transfers are parsed and loaded into staging tables; failed or incomplete transfers generate alerts; crosswalk mapping is applied; data appears in UM systems for eligibility checks,Implementations must load member data into the eligibility database and other systems as part of payer onboarding
CAGM crosswalk & group mapping,"Apply the CAGM crosswalk to map incoming LOB, group and benefit package codes to OncoHealth standard fields (e.g., InsuranceProviderID, GroupID)",Every incoming code is translated to the correct OncoHealth value according to the crosswalk; mapping is documented and tested with sample data,Crosswalk ensures BlueKC values like BKC1 and FLOB codes map consistently; derived from the provided CAGM crosswalk spreadsheet
Carve-out and secondary PBM routing logic,Develop routing logic to send pharmacy authorizations to the correct PBM when prescription benefits are carved out to a non-Optum PBM,Pharmacy authorizations follow carve-out dates: use alternate PBM when indicator is Y and date range applies; revert to Optum when indicator is N or outside carve-out dates,PBM integration tasks require awareness of carve-out indicator and dates; final PBM integration may extend beyond current scope
Eligibility API & Database setup,Load eligibility database and create an InsuranceProvider record for BlueKC (and other payers) via post-deploy script during implementation; example shows inserting BCBSKC and CAMBIA with service method bcbskc270_271,"InsuranceProvider table contains a record with ID and name for BCBSKC; fields Name='Blue Cross Blue Shield of Kansas City', ServiceMethod='bcbskc270_271', RealtimeAuthMethod='LOCAL', CreatedBy='System'; script executes without errors","This follows the eligibility-db repo post-deploy script, which adds InsuranceProvider records using a SQL insert statement; example PR shows insertion of BCBSKC and CAMBIA"
Test file analysis & mapping sign-off,"Exchange test eligibility files with BlueKC, analyse them for layout alignment, nulls and field content. Sign off on the file specification and interface agreements and produce a source-to-target mapping from raw file to Bronze/Silver/Gold/EligibilityMS layers.","Test files are reviewed; issues (misaligned field names, extra fields, nulls) are resolved; file spec and interface agreements are signed by both parties; source-to-target mapping document is completed and approved; test loads into all layers succeed.","Derived from MBR tasks: Discovery, create file spec interface agreement, receive test files, sign off file spec, create S2T mappings; data profiler report flagged field name mismatches and nulls which must be addressed."
